SELECT [s].[IdSistema], [s].[Nombre], [s].[Activo], [r].[IdRol], [r].[Nombre], [r].[Activo], [u].[Activo], [u].[EsPrincipal], [u].[IdUsuarioSistema], [t].[IdObjeto], [t].[Nombre], [t].[Tipo], [t].[Url], [t].[Titulo], [t].[Icono], [t].[Activo], [t].[Orden], [t].[IdPadre], [t].[IdRolObjeto]
FROM [UsuarioSistema] AS [u]
INNER JOIN [Sistemas] AS [s] ON [u].[SistemaId] = [s].[IdSistema]
INNER JOIN [Roles] AS [r] ON [u].[RolId] = [r].[IdRol]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [o].[IdObjeto], [o].[Nombre], [o].[Tipo], [o].[Url], [o].[Titulo], [o].[Icono], [o].[Activo], [o].[Orden], [o].[IdPadre], [r0].[IdRolObjeto], [r0].[IdRol]
    FROM [RolObjeto] AS [r0]
    INNER JOIN [Objeto] AS [o] ON [r0].[IdObjeto] = [o].[IdObjeto]
    WHERE [r0].[Activo] = CAST(1 AS bit) AND [o].[Activo] = CAST(1 AS bit)
) AS [t] ON [r].[IdRol] = [t].[IdRol]
